<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путаный.html>пу́таный</a> (15330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-аный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путаный.html>пу́таный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pútanyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пу́танее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пу́таней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tangled, interwoven</li>
<li>inconsistent, illogical, unclear, confused, difficult to understand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frivolous</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stupid</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">illogical</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивчивый.html>сби́вчивый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sbívčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нелогичный.html>нелоги́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nelogíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неясный.html>нея́сный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nejásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">frivolous</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:легкомысленный.html>легкомы́сленный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lexkomýslennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stupid</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бестолковый.html>бестолко́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bestolkóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***путать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a> (5778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">plątać</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">плутати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plutaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pútatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепутать.html>перепу́тать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">впу́тать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tangle
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mix up (with), to confuse (with)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепутать.html>перепу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perepútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to confuse
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get mixed up, to confuse
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепутать.html>перепу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perepútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to involve in, to embroil
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутать.html>запу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">впу́тать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vpútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(horses)</i> to hobble, to fetter
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***путаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́таться</a> (5836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́таться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pútatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́таться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутаться.html>спу́таться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">впу́таться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get tangled</li>
<li>to be misled, to get confused, to get mixed up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́таться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказ.html>расска́зе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pútatʹsja</b> v rasskáze</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give a confused account/story</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́таться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показание.html>показа́ниях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pútatʹsja</b> v pokazánijax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be inconsistent in one's testimony; contradict oneself in one's evidence/statement</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to interfere <i>(in)</i>, to meddle <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́таться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pútatʹsja</b> ne v svojó délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to meddle in other people's affairs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́таться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pútatʹsja</b> pod nogámi u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get under smb's feet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:путаться.html>пу́тайся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>pútajsja</b> pod nogámi!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stay out of my way!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep company <i>(with)</i>, to get mixed up <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>наш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сын</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спутаться.html>спу́тался</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> каки́ми-то <a href = vnd.unilang:уголовный.html>уголо́вными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́пами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naš syn <b>spútalsja</b> s kakími-to ugolóvnymi típami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">our son got mixed up with some criminal types</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sleep <i>(with)</i>, to go to bed <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***путешествовавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путешествовать.html>путеше́ствовавший</a> (7095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***путный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тный</a> (11555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путы.html>пу́т</a>(ь)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">put(ʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pútnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пу́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пу́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reasonable, good
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pútnyj</b> sovét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">good advice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тного</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услышать.html>услы́шишь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot nevó <b>pútnovo</b> slova ne uslýšišʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can't expect him to say anything sensible</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> worthwhile, good, decent, usable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ме</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тного</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нож.html>ножа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v dóme <b>pútnovo</b> nožá net</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there isn't a single usable knife in this house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тного</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йдет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz nevó ničevó <b>pútnovo</b> ne výjdet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you'll never make a man of him</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:путный.html>пу́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>годи́тся</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ni na što <b>pútnoje</b> ne godítsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he'll never amount to anything, he is a ne'er-do-well</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***путь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a> (284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pǫtь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*pont-</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*pint-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*p(o)nt-h₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">putʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>way, path, road
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> петербу́рг.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>po putí</b> v Peterbúrg.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He’s <b>on his way to</b> St. Petersburg.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружный.html>кружно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kružnój <b>putʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">roundabout way</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prokládyvatʹ/proložítʹ putʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make <b>a path/road</b>; break <b>a trail</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>track, line</li>
<li>means</li>
<li>trip, journey</li>
<li>route</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пух</a> (6945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пухъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puxŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*puxъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пух</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pux</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пу́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пу́хи</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пу́хов</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>down (feathers)</li>
<li>fluff</li></ol>

***пухлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пухлый.html>пу́хлый</a> (6276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*puxlъ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пух</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pux</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fluff, originally breath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пухнуть.html>пу́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">púxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пухлый.html>пу́хлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púxlyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пухле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пухле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plump, chubby</li>
<li>swollen, puffy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пухнуть.html>пу́хнуть</a> (26192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*puxnǫti</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пухнуть.html>пу́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распухнуть.html>распу́хнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опухнуть.html>опу́хнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспухнуть.html>вспу́хнуть</a></b>)

***пуховый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуховый.html>пухо́вый</a> (14317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пух</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pux</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуховый.html>пухо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">puxóvyj</span>)
</p>

***пучина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пучина.html>пучи́на</a> (14748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучина.html>пучи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pučína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучина.html>пучи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучина.html>пучи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучина.html>пучи́н</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучок.html>пучо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pučók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучок.html>пучка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучок.html>пучки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пучок.html>пучко́в</a></b>)

***пушистый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стый</a> (5470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pušístyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>furry (covered with fur), fluffy, light, airy, fuzzy</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pušístyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стых</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушистый.html>пуши́стая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mascot (person in a furry animal suit)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушка</a> (8581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Common Slavic. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пушька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pušĭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, further etymology is disputed:
</p>
<ul><li>Vasmer: borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">buhsa</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">puška</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">puszka</i>, from Vulgar <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">buxis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πυξίς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puxís</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Initial <b>п-</b> is of Bavarian origin.</li>
<li>Černyh: possibly from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*пущька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*puščĭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пущати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puščati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw projectiles; to fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. On the basis of West Slavic (and partly South Slavic) this word hybridized with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">buhsa</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">buška</i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушка.html>пу́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gun, cannon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">90-мм <a href = vnd.unilang:зенитный.html>зени́тная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">90-mm zenítnaja <b>púška</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">90-mm anti-aircraft <b>gun</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автоматический.html>автомати́ческая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">avtomatíčeskaja <b>púška</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">auto<b>cannon</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gun, handgun</li>
<li>hoax <i>(informal)</i></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>In modern military usage, <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушка</a> refers to an artillery piece with a relatively long barrel, operating with a relatively low angle of fire or as a direct fire weapon, e.g. a field gun, an anti-aircraft gun, or an autocannon.
</p><p>Historically, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушка</a> had been used to refer to any large artillery piece, similarly to the historical usage of the English word cannon.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушечный.html>пу́шечный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">púšečnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пушка́рь</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">puškárʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пушкинский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушкинский.html>пу́шкинский</a> (6349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пу́шкин</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Púškin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушкинский.html>пу́шкинский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púškinskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Pushkin <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">Russian surname, especially referring to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pushkin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Pushkin">Alexander Pushkin</a>, Russian poet, novelist and playwright</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; Pushkin's

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушо́к</a> (2409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пух.html>пух</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pux</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pušók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушко́в</a></b>)

<ol><li>down</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуща.html>пу́ща</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pušča</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">desolate place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*puťa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pȗstъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">desolate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пусто́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пущий.html>пу́щий</a> (20318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Adjective formed from the comparative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуща.html>пу́ще</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">púšče</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">greater</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больший.html>бо́льший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bólʹšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бо́льше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bólʹše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пущий.html>пу́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púščij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> greater
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пуща.html>пу́щей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:важность.html>ва́жности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>púščej</b> vážnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in order to appear more important</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">for <b>greater</b> importance</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bьčela</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пчела.html>пчела́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pčelá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пчела.html>пчелы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пчела.html>пчёлы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пчела.html>пчёл</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пшеница.html>пшени́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pšeníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пшеница.html>пшени́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пшеница.html>пшени́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пшеница.html>пшени́ц</a></b>)
